<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crupen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*crūpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kreupaną</i>.

***kruis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruis.html>kruis</a> (2711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cruce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crux</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruis.html>kruis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruizen.html>kruizen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisen.html>kruisen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisje.html>kruisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cross
<ol><li>X-shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> such shape as used in heraldry</li>
<li>execution device with such shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> difficult or tortuous situation</li></ol></li>
<li>crotch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sharp</li>
<li>heads <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">side of a coin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***kruisbes.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruisbes.html>kruisbes</a> (128177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisbes.html>kruisbes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisbessen.html>kruisbessen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisbes.html>kruisbesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">gooseberry</span> or the gooseberry plant, <i>Ribes uva-crispa</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kruisbei</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kruisbezie</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crucen</i>. ***kruislings.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruislings.html>kruislings</a> (64331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruis.html>kruis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lings</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ly, -wise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***kruistocht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruistocht.html>kruistocht</a> (12919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruis.html>kruis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">journey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in 1700.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruistocht.html>kruistocht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruistochten.html>kruistochten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruistocht.html>kruistochtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crusade, a Christian holy war</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quest, 'sacred' cause, notably against some evil</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisvaart.html>kruisvaart</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruisen.html>kruisen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruistocht.html>kruistocht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruistochten.html>kruistochten</a></b>)
</p>

***krul.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krul.html>krul</a> (49130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crulle</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kruzlǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> curled</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pre-Germanic" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pre-Germanic">Pre-Germanic</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grus-</i>, contracted from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gurus-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twist, curl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, same source as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">گرس</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gors</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">braid of hair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krul.html>krul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krullen.html>krullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krul.html>krulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A curl (in hair or writing).</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:curly.html>curly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a> as a symbol, used by teachers to mark answers as correct.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music<span class="ib-comma">,</span> lutherie</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A scroll <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">e.g. of a violin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krullen.html>krullen</a> (11744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crullen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krul.html>krul</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:krullen.html>krullen</a></b>
</p>

<ol><li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a>) spiraalvormig <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krullen.html>krulde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> krultang.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***kryptonite.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kryptonite.html>kryptonite</a> (49128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a fictional radioactive element, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kryptonite" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kryptonite"><a href = vnd.unilang:kryptonite.html>kryptonite</a></a>, that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a detrimental effect on the otherwise invulnerable character <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Superman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Superman"><a href = vnd.unilang:superman.html>Superman</a></a>. Apparently formed as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:krypton.html>krypton</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a chemical element, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kr.html>Kr</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ite</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kryptonite.html>kryptonite</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>

***kuchen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kuchen.html>kuchen</a> (40602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cuchen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coechen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cochen</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kuh-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, likely of onomatopoeic origin. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cough</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">keuchen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuchen.html>kuchen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to give out a dry and <a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>brief</a> cough</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***kuiken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kuiken.html>kuiken</a> (25287)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kuken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kiken</i>, originally from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kiukīną</i>. A modern variant form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kieken</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Küken</i> (from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span></span>) and English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chicken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuiken.html>kuiken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuikens.html>kuikens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuikentje.html>kuikentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chick, the hatched young of a bird, especially fowl</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kuiken.html>kuiken</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***kuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kuis.html>kuis</a> (20533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cuusch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chaste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">conscius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">conscious</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">com-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scire</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">conscious</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">keusch</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cul</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kul</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">testicle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">coille</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōleus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">testicle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">testicle</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">marble</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small ball used in various games</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:loser.html>loser</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">wuss</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">wimp</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Clipping of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauwekul.html>flauwekul</a></i>, a compound of the adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauw.html>flauw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">insipid, tasteless</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kul</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">testicle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">nonsense</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rubbish</span></li></ol>

***kumquat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kumquat.html>kumquat</a> (56929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">柑橘</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gam1 gwat1</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">金橘</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gam1 gwat1</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">golden <a href = vnd.unilang:tangerine.html>tangerine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">loquat</i> – same second character.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kumquat.html>kumquat</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kumquats</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small, orange citrus-like fruit which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> native to Asia (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Citrus_japonica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Citrus japonica"><i>Citrus japonica</i></a></span>, syn. <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Fortunella_japonica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Fortunella japonica"><i>Fortunella japonica</i></a></span>).</li></ol>

***kun.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> (268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">second-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></i></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Can you do something for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>As <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usual in Dutch, the <i>-t</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dropped when the pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i> immediately follows the verb. However, unlike for all other verbs, the form that results <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not identical to the first-person singular, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></i>. The form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also frequently used, by analogy with regular verbs, but it may be considered nonstandard by some.
</p>

</p>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopt.html>klopt</a>?</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunde.html>kunde</a> (34100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">conde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cunde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kundi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kundīn</i>. Maybe related to from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵneh₃-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunde.html>kunde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunde.html>kundes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>skill, competency</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> (89)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">connen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cunnen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cunnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kunnaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵneh₃-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be possible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> not <b>possible</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> can, to be able to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:getraind.html>getraind</a> sportbeoefenaar <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>could</b> run well, because he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a trained <a href = vnd.unilang:sportsman.html>sportsman</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may, can, to be allowed to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You <b>can</b> always call <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> can go, to be able to go, can get
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> in!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>can</b>not <b>get</b> into my house anymore!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be able to do, to be capable of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>am</b> not <b>able</b> to do that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be available (for any type of meeting or appointment)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> morgenavond <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I will not <b>be available</b> tomorrow night.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***kunst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a> (1715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cunst</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">const</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cunste</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">conste</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skill, ability, knowledge, craft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge, know-how, skill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kunstiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge, ability</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǴenH-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵnō-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-st</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skill, wisdom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge, wisdom, skill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">konst</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">kenst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">cunning</span>.
</p>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">art</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">work</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>

***kurgan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a> (64321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">курга́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurgán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span></span> language (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kurgans</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A prehistoric burial mound once used by peoples in Siberia and Central Asia.
<ul><li><b>2004</b>, Benjamin Fortson, <i>Indo-European Language and Culture</i>, Blackwell, 2005, p. 41
<dl><dd>The <b>kurgans</b> and the burials they contain are consistent with the early <a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>Ie</a> burial practices outlined above, and the late Lithuanian archaeologist Marija Gimbutas proposed that the <a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a> peoples <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> in fact early Indo-Europeans.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Philip L. <a href = vnd.unilang:kohl.html>Kohl</a>, <i>Chapter 6: The Maikop Singularity: The Unequal Accumulation of Wealth on the Bronze Age Eurasian <a href = vnd.unilang:steppe.html>Steppe</a>?</i>, Bryan K. <a href = vnd.unilang:hanks.html>Hanks</a>, Katheryn M. Linduff (<a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>), <i>Social Complexity in Prehistoric Eurasia: Monuments, Metals and Mobility</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=fEK-BkqXfJACamp;pg=PA91amp;dq=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;f=false">page 91</a>,
<dl><dd>In 1897 N. I. Veselovskii excavated the very large, nearly 11 <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> high Oshad <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></b> or barrow in the town of Maikop in the Kuban region near the foothills of the northwestern Caucasus (the present-day capital of the Adygei Republic).<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>This discovery stimulated the excavation of other large <b>kurgans</b> located in the same general region, some of which seemed royal-like in their dimensions and, when not robbed in antiquity, in their materials.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, David W. Anthony, <i>The Horse, the Wheel, and Language: How Bronze-Age <a href = vnd.unilang:riders.html>Riders</a> from the Eurasian <a href = vnd.unilang:steppes.html>Steppes</a> Shaped the Modern World</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=0FDqf415wqgCamp;pg=PA329amp;dq=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;f=false">page 329</a>,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> in the middle Volga region some <b>kurgans</b> have central graves containing <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a> females, as at Krasnosamarskoe IV.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>The appearance of <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a> females in one out of five <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></b> graves, including central graves, suggests that gender <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not the only factor that determined who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> buried under a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">burial mound</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">barrow</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tumulus</span></li></ul>
</body>

***kurkdroog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kurkdroog.html>kurkdroog</a> (39314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurk.html>kurk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droog.html>droog</a></i>. First attested in the eighteenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurkdroog.html>kurkdroog</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bone-dry</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">very dry</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">beendroog</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">gortdroog</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurkdroog.html>kurkdroog</a></b>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a> (1318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kussaz</i>. The older Dutch forms with -u- are <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> from the verb, those with -o- derive directly from the noun. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kuss</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kiss</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">kys</i>.
</p>

***kussen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a> (1475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cussen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kussijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kiss, to give a kiss to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kuste.html>kuste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zachtjes.html>zachtjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wang.html>wang</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>kissed</b> him gently on the cheek.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to practice kissing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>Niemand</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kust.html>kust</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Nobody <b>kisses</b> better than he.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cussin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cuisin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cussin</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussens.html>kussens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussentje.html>kussentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
